a = {'Id': 0,'fname': 1, 'lname': 2, 'income': 3}

n = int(input())
Bureau = []
s = 0
count = 0
for i in range(0,n):
    data = list(input().split(','))
    data[b['fname']] = data[b['fname']].lower().copy()
    data[b['lname']] = data[b['lname']].lower().copy()
    spend = data[b['annual spend']]
    if(len(spend)>=1 and spend[0] != '-'):
        s = s + int(spend)
        count = count + 1
    Bureau.append(data)

avg_spend = float(s/count)

def Search(app):
    for i in range(0, n):
        data = Bureau[i]
        if(app[a['fname']]==data[b['fname']] and app[a['lname']]==data[b['lname']]):
            return i
    return -1

def Rule1(app, index):
    data = Bureau[index]
    c1 = int(data[b['total assets']]) > int(data[b['total liability']])
    c2 = int(data[b['bureau score']]) > 50
    c3 = (int(data[b['annual spend']])/int(app[a['income']])) > 0.1
    c4 = int(data[b['annual spend']]) > avg_spend
    return (c1 and c2 and c3 and c4)

def Rule2(app, index):
    data = Bureau[index]
    c1 = int(data[b['total assets']]) > int(data[b['total liability']])
    c2 = data[b['home ownership flag']] == '1'
    c3 = int(data[b['bureau score']]) > 30
    c4 = int(data[b['annual spend']])/int(app[a['income']]) > 0.1
    c5 = int(data[b['annual spend']]) > avg_spend
    return (c1 and c2 and c3 and c4 and c5)
    
m = int(input())
for i in range(0, m):
    application = list(input().split(','))
    application[a['fname']] = application[a['fname']].lower.copy()
    application[a['lname']] = application[a['lname']].lower.copy()
    index = Search(application)
    r1 = False
    r2 = False
    if (index != -1):
        r1 = Rule1(application, index)
        r2 = Rule2(application, index)
    if (r1==True or r2==True):
        print(application[a['Id']]+',Yes')
    else:
        print(application[a['Id']]+',No')

This is to inform  that the Ministry of Heavy Industries, Government of India has supported the Technology Innovation Platforms (TIPs) for promoting the innovation in manufacturing through the collaboration of the experts (academia and Industry), entrepreneurs, start ups and students in the country.

As a part of these platforms, the students of engineering degree programs are given an opportunity to work on practically relevant problems at four different institutions: AMTDC-IITM, ARAI, CMTI, and ICAT  through an internship program. We will appreciate if you can publicise the internship opportunity to the students of your Institution/College through email or otherwise.

Strong abstract reasoning and problem solving skills. Must be able to produce clean and efficient code and should have done a lot of programming/coding(any language). Strong fundamentals in DSA and must have experience in writing complex algorithms. 

Job Designation                 : Software Development Intern
CTC Offered -36.5 lpa

Stipend 1,50,000 p.m.

Coding Test followed by Criteria Cognitive Aptitude Test(CCAT)

Round2 :- Technical Interview

After clearing both rounds, candidates will be facing a 3rd round which will be disclosed later.

*INSTRUCTIONS FOR STUDENTS*

Test 1: Online Coding Test

Date: Thursday 29th July 2021 
Time: 4:00 PM ( login window will be open only for 30 mins )
Duration: 90 mins
Format: 3 competitive programming questions
How to proceed: test link will be mailed 12 hours before the test (check spam folder as well). Contact your placement team if you have not received the link
Test 2: Online CCAT

Date: Thursday 29th July 2021 
Time: 6:00 PM ( can attempt the test anytime before  30th July 2021 6:00 AM  )
Duration: 15 mins per attempt ( 2 attempts per candidate)
Format: 50 aptitude questions 
Cutoff Required: 45/50
How to proceed: The test link will be mailed after you complete the Coding test (check the spam folder as well). Contact your placement team if you have not received the link
*PLEASE NOTE: If you have attempted CCAT once before in the last 6 months, you will be eligible for only 1 more attempt. If you have given CCAT twice before in the last 6 months, you will not be eligible for any more attempts*
